THE LAND ACQUISITION ACT (CHAPTER 460)
Declaration under Section 5
I, Janaka Bandara Thennakoon, Minister of Lands and Land
Development, hereby declare under Sub-section (1) of Section 5 of
the Land Acquisition Act, that the lands described below are needed
for a public purpose and will be acquired under the provisions of
that Act.
The allotments of below mentioned lands in total extent of about
22.4969 Hectares, depicted in Advance Tracing No.H/RDA/SEW/
2014/19, prepared by the Senior Surveyor-General of Hambantota
District, situated in the  Villages of  Mahapalassa and Viharagama in
Grama Niladhari Division of Mahapalassa and Viharagama  in the
Minor Division of Magampattuwa in the Divisional Secretary’s
Division of  Sooriyawewa in Hambantota District in Southern
Province and bounded as follows:
1. Lot ‘A’ – Bogahayaya – Extent: 0.0046 Hectare
North: Bogahayaya claimed by G . Hiruni Mihirawi; East:
Bogahayaya claimed by G . Hiruni Mihirawi and Lot C; South:
Lots C and B; West: Lot B, Bogahayaya claimed by G. Hiruni Mihirawi
and Bogahayaya claimed by E.G . Dharmasena.

claimed by G . Hiruni Mihirawi and Lot A; East: Lots A and C; South:
Lot C; West: Lot C and Bogahayaya claimed by E.G . Dharmasena.

the Land Acquisition Act, that the lands described below are needed
for a public purpose and will be acquired under the provisions of
that Act.

–––––––––––––––––––––––––
THE LAND ACQUISITION ACT (CHAPTER 460)
Declaration under Section 5
I, Janaka Bandara Thennakoon, Minister of Lands and Land
Development, hereby declare under Sub-section (1) of Section 5
of the Land Acquisition Act, that the lands described below are
needed for a public purpose and will be acquired under the provisions
of that Act.
The boundaries of the lands of  24.7726 Hectares in extent, indicated
in the Progression Tracing bearing number H/SRY/2012/767 dated
31.01.2013 prepared by the Surveyor-General, is situated in the
Villages of Beddawewa, Nabadagaswewa, Mahaara,  Buruthakanda
and Nugekanda in the Sooriyawewa Divisional Secretary’s Division
in Hambantota District in the Southern Province.
1. Lot ‘A’ – Palugahahena – Extent: 0.0041 Hectare
